## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the rate of change of concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and concentration in a chemical reaction. This is a classic chemical kinetics problem where the rate law relates the reaction rate to the concentration of reactants, potentially with various orders and mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Zero-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0', 'scenario': 'Constant rate independent of concentration, e.g., surface-catalyzed reactions at saturation'}
- {'name': 'First-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to concentration, radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition'}
- {'name': 'Second-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Bimolecular reaction where two molecules of same species react'}
- {'name': 'nth-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1', 'scenario': 'General power-law rate expression for fractional or arbitrary reaction order'}
- {'name': 'Reversible first-order reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1', 'scenario': 'First-order forward and reverse reactions approaching equilibrium'}
- {'name': 'Reversible reaction with equilibrium', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * (A - c1)', 'scenario': 'Net rate proportional to displacement from equilibrium concentration'}
- {'name': 'Mixed-order / competing reactions', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Parallel first- and second-order reaction pathways'}
- {'name': 'Saturation kinetics (Michaelis-Menten-like)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme-catalyzed or surface-limited reactions with substrate saturation'}
- {'name': 'Substrate inhibition kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme kinetics with substrate inhibition at high concentrations'}
- {'name': 'Autocatalytic reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A)', 'scenario': 'Reaction where product catalyzes the conversion, logistic-type rate'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent rate (photochemical)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Reactions with time-varying external influence like light intensity'}
- {'name': 'Consecutive reaction intermediate', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) + c2 * exp(c3 * t)', 'scenario': 'Rate of intermediate species in consecutive A→B→C reactions'}
- {'name': 'Power-law with offset', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2', 'scenario': 'nth-order kinetics with a constant source or sink term'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative rate (consumption) proportional to concentration power → Power-law rate expression dA_dt = -k * A**n indicating reaction order n
- Rate approaching zero at a nonzero concentration → Reversible reaction with equilibrium, suggests (A - A_eq) terms
- Rate that increases then decreases with concentration → Substrate inhibition or autocatalytic mechanism with A/(1+A+A²) or A*(K-A) structure
- Exponential time dependence in rate → Suggests the system is being driven by time-varying conditions or the rate is derived from an integrated first-order process
- Linear relationship between dA_dt and A → First-order kinetics; slope gives rate constant, intercept indicates reversibility or constant source
- Curvature in log(|dA_dt|) vs log(A) plot → Indicates fractional or non-integer reaction order, use A**c form
- Rate proportional to product of concentration and remaining capacity → Autocatalytic or logistic kinetics A*(c-A)
- Constant rate at high concentration transitioning to concentration-dependent at low → Saturation kinetics with rational fraction structure
